<Name>Bezimienny -</Name><time>1533850893821</time><Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
Amazing. Donuts. It's no joke that they sell out fast by the time it's past noon--so if you want to try out the popular ones (H&C croissants), you'll have to arrive early.

Despite that, however, I was pleasantly surprised that the donuts--especially the twisted kind--were very soft. I only managed to snag 2 before it went out.

The owner there is also friendly; she told me about how her husband makes them for about 30 years now. Wow.

tl; dr ++++Amazing donuts, long-running service</Text>

<resp>None< /resp>< text>
Expensive, the potato tacos were so greasy and overflowing with mushrooms and other veggies they looked like an undercooked enchilada pie that had been dropped a few times and with extra frying oil on top. No real discernable tortilla to pick up, a total mess and not very tasty. I drove out of the way because they had potato tacos and was disappointed. Not going to give any place 2 stars because of one food item or one bad experience with an employee, though. The Carne Asada and Carnitas tacos were also expensive and not very good. The meat was chewy and flavorless. So why give them 2 stars rather than 1? The customer service, their fish taco and the chips and salsa were all very good. I would go there again for those and save the $40 I spent on the other tacos.</text>

< rate>
5</rate>
< review>
I found Lupe's first at their Dana Point location and fell in love, so I was very happy to try this location as well. The line can get long around lunch time but ordering ahead is always possible and even then the wait is worth it. The menu options are deep and diverse, with a lot of options that are perfectly suited for Instagram style posts like the Flaming Hot Cheeto burrito (a must try!) or the California Burrito. It's basically the same as everywhere else, but better. I recommend switching it up and getting it with the Al Pastor they have roasting on a spit all day.

The tacos are also great, with a variety of specialty options that you won't find anywhere else as well as traditional street tacos you can get for cheap. Again I have to recommend that Al Pastor, it's unreal how flavorful it can be without too much grease like a lot of places. And if you like it spicy, be sure to get the habanero salsa on the side because it's amazing and actually spicy. I know lots of places will say they have something spicy and when you try it you just go "Meh, I mean it's kinda spicy" but that salsas is actually spicy and delicious and I put it on way more than just Lupe's.< /review>
